				<div  class="module post-module et_pb_extra_module  et_pb_posts_0" style="border-top-color:#db509f">
	<div class="module-head">
		<h1 style="color:#db509f">Project Management Career</h1>
		<span class="module-filter">Latest</span>
	</div>
		<div class="main-post">
		<article id="post-3387" class="post-3387 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-project-management-career tag-project-management-activities tag-project-management-process tag-project-manager-activities et-has-post-format-content et_post_format-et-post-format-standard">
			<div class="header">
			<a href="https://gjc.mbc.mybluehost.me/successful-project-manager/" title="5 Critical Skills Every Successful Project Manager Should Have" class="featured-image">
				<img src="https://i0.wp.com/gjc.mbc.mybluehost.me/wp-content/uploads/2023/04/Creative-Marketing-Project-Manager-resume-8.jpg?resize=627%2C376&amp;ssl=1" alt="5 Critical Skills Every Successful Project Manager Should Have" /><span class="et_pb_extra_overlay"></span>
			</a><span class="score-bar" style="width:98%;background-color:#db509f;"><span class="score-text">Score 98%</span></span>			</div>
			<div class="post-content">
								<h2 class="entry-title"><a class="et-accent-color" style="color:#db509f;" href="https://gjc.mbc.mybluehost.me/successful-project-manager/">5 Critical Skills Every Successful Project Manager Should Have</a></h2>
				<div class="post-meta vcard">
					<p>by <a href="https://gjc.mbc.mybluehost.me/author/vijay0015/" class="url fn" title="Posts by Vijay Kumar, PMP" rel="author">Vijay Kumar, PMP</a> | <span class="updated">Sep 11, 2023</span> | <a href="https://gjc.mbc.mybluehost.me/project-management-career/" rel="tag">Project Management Career</a> | <a class="comments-link" href="https://gjc.mbc.mybluehost.me/successful-project-manager/#comments">0 <span title="comment count" class="comment-bubble post-meta-icon"></span></a> | <span class="rating-stars" title="Rating: 0.00"><span class="post-meta-icon rating-star rating-star-empty rating-star-1"></span>
<span class="post-meta-icon rating-star rating-star-empty rating-star-2"></span>
<span class="post-meta-icon rating-star rating-star-empty rating-star-3"></span>
<span class="post-meta-icon rating-star rating-star-empty rating-star-4"></span>
<span class="post-meta-icon rating-star rating-star-empty rating-star-5"></span>
</span></p>
				</div>
								<div class="excerpt entry-summary">
									<p>Project management is a complex task that requires a combination of skills, experience, and expertise. A successful project manager should have strong leadership, time management, communication, risk management, and negotiation skills. These critical skills can significantly increase the chances of project success and ensure that projects are delivered on time, within budget, and to the desired quality standards. With the right balance of these skills, project managers can achieve exceptional results, earn clients' trust, and build lasting relationships with team members and stakeholders.</p>
								</div>
			</div>
		</article>
	</div>
